## Multilens Translation Atlas

### AQM

- `P1`
  Equation:

  \[\rho_{\mathrm{P1}}^+ = \Phi_{\mathrm{P1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}}(\rho_{\mathrm{P1}}^-), \qquad \Phi_{\mathrm{P1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} = \mathsf O_{\texttt{dalm-}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{otaly}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{sholy}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{chofchol}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{otoralchy}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{shopchy}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{cholfy}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{kor}}\]

  Variable legend: `rho^-` incoming folio line state; `rho^+` outgoing line state; `Phi_line^(AQM)` source operator chain.
  Reading: temporal drive / structure matrix / fluid medium line.
  Confidence: strong

- `P2`

### Game Theory

- `P1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: temporal drive / structure matrix / fluid medium line.
  Confidence: strong

\[\Phi_j^{(\mathrm{CUT})} = T_{\mathrm{CUT}}^{-1} \Phi_j^{(\mathrm{AQM})} T_{\mathrm{CUT}}, \qquad \Phi_j^{(\mathrm{phys})} = T_{\mathrm{phys}}^{-1} \Phi_j^{(\mathrm{AQM})} T_{\mathrm{phys}}\]

\[\rho_* = (\Psi_n \circ \cdots \circ \Psi_1)(\rho_0)\]
